  var xda_ad_free = (function() {
    var getCookie = function(name, value) {
      if (document.cookie.indexOf(name) == 0) //Match without a ';' if its the firs
        return -1 < document.cookie.indexOf(value ? name + "=" + value + ";" : name + "=")
      else if (value && document.cookie.indexOf("; " + name + "=" + value) + name.length + value.length + 3 == document.cookie.length) //match without an ending ';' if its the last
          return true
      else { //match cookies in the middle with 2 ';' if you want to check for a value
        return -1 < document.cookie.indexOf("; " + (value ? name + "=" + value + ";" : name + "="))
      }
    };

    return getCookie("bbxuvuktynom", '1');
  })();

<script>

var xda_ad_choice = (function() {
  var rand = function(min, max) {
    return Math.random() * (max - min) + min;
  };
   
  var getRandomItem = function(list, weight) {
    var total_weight = weight.reduce(function (prev, cur, i, arr) {
        return prev + cur;
    });
     
    var random_num = rand(0, total_weight);
    var weight_sum = 0;
     
    for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
      weight_sum += weight[i];
      weight_sum = +weight_sum.toFixed(2);
       
      if (random_num <= weight_sum) {
        return list[i];
      }
    }
  };
   
  var list = ['purch', 'sortable'];
  var weight = [1.00, 0.00];
  var random_item = getRandomItem(list, weight);
  
  return random_item;
})();

//xda_ad_choice = "purch";

if (location.hash == "#xda_ad_test") {
  xda_ad_choice = "sortable";
}
</script>

<script>
                    var getCookie = function(name, value) {
                        if (document.cookie.indexOf(name) == 0) //Match without a ';' if its the firs
                            return -1 < document.cookie.indexOf(value ? name + "=" + value + ";" : name + "=")
                        else if (value && document.cookie.indexOf("; " + name + "=" + value) + name.length + value.length + 3 == document.cookie.length) //match without an ending ';' if its the last
                            return true
                        else { //match cookies in the middle with 2 ';' if you want to check for a value
                            return -1 < document.cookie.indexOf("; " + (value ? name + "=" + value + ";" : name + "="))
                        }
                    };

                    if(!(getCookie('subscriberemailauth') || getCookie('subscriberemailauth'))) { // not authenticated, show subscribe form
                        document.getElementById('newsletter-sidebar-subscribe').style.display = 'block';
                    } else { // does have newsletter cookie
                        let subscribeForm = document.getElementsByClassName('newsletters-subscribe-form')
                        if (subscribeForm) {
                            subscribeForm[0].style.display = 'none';
                        }

                    }

<script>
        //Fixes for articles that had their disqus ID's erroneously merged - @see also news-single.php
        var disqusFixes = [
            {'original':'122995 http://www.xda-developers.com/?p=122995', 'new':'122995-2 http://www.xda-developers.com/?p=122995'},
            {'original':'122998 http://www.xda-developers.com/?p=122998', 'new':'122998-2 http://www.xda-developers.com/?p=122998'}
        ];
        jQuery('span.dsq-postid').each(function() {
             if ( jQuery(this).attr('data-dsqidentifier')) {
                var curdisqusID = jQuery(this).data('dsqidentifier');

                for (var i=0;i<disqusFixes.length;i++) {
                    if (curdisqusID === disqusFixes[i].original) {
                        //Need to directly modify the attribute of the html as disqus reads this and not jquery's data structure
                        jQuery(this).attr('data-dsqidentifier', disqusFixes[i].new);
                    }
                }
            }
        });

        var forumThreadIDs = [];
        var commentType = '';

        jQuery('a.xda-forum-link').each(function() {
            var xdathreadid = jQuery(this).attr('data-thread-id');
            if (xdathreadid.length > 0) {
                forumThreadIDs.push('threadid[]=' + xdathreadid);
                jQuery(this).attr('id', 'forumlink-' + xdathreadid);

            }

            if (forumThreadIDs.length > 0) {
                commentType = 'sidebar';
            }
        });

        jQuery('span.xda-forum-link-2').each(function() {
            var xdathreadid = jQuery(this).attr('data-thread-id');
            if (xdathreadid.length > 0) {
                forumThreadIDs.push('threadid[]=' + xdathreadid);
                jQuery(this).attr('id', 'forumlink-' + xdathreadid);
            }

            if (forumThreadIDs.length > 0) {
                commentType = 'archive';
            }
        });
        
        jQuery('a.xda-forum-link-home').each(function() {
           var xdathreadid = jQuery(this).attr('data-thread-id');
            if (xdathreadid.length > 0) {
                forumThreadIDs.push('threadid[]=' + xdathreadid);
                jQuery(this).attr('id', 'forumlink-' + xdathreadid);
            }

            if (forumThreadIDs.length > 0) {
                commentType = 'home';
            }
        });

        var forumThreadIDQueryString = forumThreadIDs.join('&');

        if (forumThreadIDQueryString.length > 0) {
            jQuery.getJSON(forum_api_url + "/threads/threadinfo?" + forumThreadIDQueryString, function(r) {
                if (typeof r.results == 'undefined') {
                    r.results = [];
                    r.results[0] = r;
                }
                
                if (r.results.length > 0) {
                    for(i=0; i < r.results.length; i++) {
                        if (commentType == 'sidebar') {
                            var forumlinkURL = jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).attr('href');
                            jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).parent().siblings('.item_meta').append('<span class="meta_comments"><a href="'+ forumlinkURL + '">' + r.results[i].replycount + ' Posts</a></span>');
                        } else if (commentType == 'archive') {
                            var forumlinkURL = jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).data('forum-url');
                            jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).html('<a href="'+ forumlinkURL + '">' + r.results[i].replycount + ' Posts</a>');
                        } else if (commentType == 'home') {
                            var forumlinkURL = jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).attr('href');
                            jQuery('#forumlink-' + r.results[i].threadid).parent().siblings('.thumb_meta').html('<span class="comments"><a href="'+ forumlinkURL + '">' + r.results[i].replycount + ' Posts</a></span>');
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>
